Staff are friendly and sincere, although possibly a little rusty due to previous covid closure ‚Äî different staff told us different stories regarding the airconditioning situation. 

The room was too warm (in spring) and after some to and fro with different staff it was finally explained that the temperature was centrally controlled so we could not adjust anything and could only open the one window in the room, which increased the runway noise. Also, the power would go off after a while ‚Äî this happened multiple times throughout the night (while we were eating dinner haha) so I think it was designed this way. Subway station is connected to the airport, but the city centre is about 1.5hrs away. That‚Äôs 3hrs travelling to and fro if you are planning on any sightseeing. There are some eateries at the airport if 3hrs is too much subway for you.
